Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-23 09:42:46]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,

                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id

[2018-12-23 09:43:16]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-23 09:48:03]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-23 09:48:35]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-23 09:53:46]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-12-23 09:54:35]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT IFNULL( CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-',  LPAD(  SUBSTRING_INDEX(MAX(outbound_no),'-',-1) + 1 ,5,REPEAT('0', 5))), CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-',  CONCAT( REPEAT('0', 5-1),'1')    )) AS outbound_no  FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE YEAR(created_date) = YEAR(NOW()) ORDER BY outbound_no desc limit 0,1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-23 09:58:22]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-23 10:19:50]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

						  outbound_no		
						, date_format(outbound_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as outbound_date	
						, client_id
						, employer_id
						, attention_to
						, email_content
						, email
						, attachment
						, concat('http://127.0.0.1/mspdoc_bare/services/files/', 'outbound_document', '/',outbound_no, '/') as filepath
						, remarks
						, approvals
						, status_id
						, ctg_id
						, amount
						, notes
						, is_active
						, date_format(created_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as created_date
						, created_by
						, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name			
					 FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE outbound_no = 'MSP18-00002'

                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-23 10:29:58]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT 
						  outbound_no		
						, date_format(outbound_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as outbound_date	
						, client_id
						, employer_id
						, attention_to
						, email_content
						, email
						, attachment
						, concat('http://127.0.0.1/mspdoc_bare/services/files/', 'outbound_document', '/',outbound_no, '/') as filepath
						, remarks
						, approvals
						, status_id
						, ctg_id
						, amount
						, notes
						, is_active
						, date_format(created_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as created_date
						, created_by
						, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name			
					 FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE outbound_no = 'MSP18-00002'

                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id

Function Details: db_query_list

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date

				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by

						  outbound_no		
						, date_format(outbound_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as outbound_date	
						, client_id
						, employer_id
						, attention_to
						, email_content
						, email
						, attachment
						, concat('http://127.0.0.1/mspdoc_bare/services/files/', 'outbound_document', '/',outbound_no, '/') as filepath
						, remarks
						, approvals
						, status_id
						, ctg_id
						, amount
						, notes
						, is_active

						, created_by
						, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name			
					 FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE outbound_no = 'MSP18-00002'

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query
 Param Details:

[2018-12-23 11:03:41]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT IFNULL( CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-',  LPAD(  SUBSTRING_INDEX(MAX(outbound_no),'-',-1) + 1 ,5,REPEAT('0', 5))), CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-',  CONCAT( REPEAT('0', 5-1),'1')    )) AS outbound_no  FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE YEAR(created_date) = YEAR(NOW()) ORDER BY outbound_no desc limit 0,1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 16 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT IFNULL( CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-',  LPAD(  SUBSTRING_INDEX(MAX(doc_no),'-',-1) + 1 ,5,REPEAT('0', 5))), CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-',  CONCAT( REPEAT('0', 5-1),'1')    )) AS doc_no  FROM cms_document_archiving WHERE YEAR(created_date) = YEAR(NOW()) ORDER BY doc_no desc limit 0,1

[2018-12-23 11:11:49]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks

				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id

				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 16 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: get_document_archiving_list

[2018-12-23 15:01:48]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details :

[2018-12-23 15:01:54]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT 
						  doc_no		
						, date_format(doc_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as doc_date	
						, client_id
						, employer_id
						, doc_type
						, date_format(from_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as from_date	
						, date_format(to_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as to_date	
						, notify
						, date_format(notify_by,'%d-%m-%Y') as notify_by	
						, notify_email
						, attachment
						, concat('http://127.0.0.1/mspdoc_bare/services/files/', 'doc_archiving', '/',doc_no, '/') as filepath
						, remarks
						, notes
						, approvals
						, status_id						
						, is_active
						, date_format(created_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as created_date
						, created_by	
						, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name			
					 FROM cms_document_archiving WHERE doc_no = 'MSP18-00001'

[2018-12-23 21:42:04]
Function Details: get_mail_signature 
 Param Details : 
"sancheev@msphitect.com.my"


[2018-12-23 21:42:04]
Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_employees.name, cms_master_employer.mail_signature, 
									cms_employees.device_info, cms_employees.device_id
									FROM cms_employees
									LEFT JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
									WHERE cms_employees.office_email in('sancheev@msphitect.com.my') AND cms_employees.is_active = 1


[2018-12-23 21:42:04]
Function Details: send_appt_reminder_email 
 Param Details : 
"sancheev@msphitect.com.my"


[2018-12-23 21:42:29]
Function Details: send_notification_archiving 
 Param Details : 
[]


[2018-12-23 21:42:29]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT date_format(cms_document_archiving.notify_by,'%d-%b-%Y %h:%i %p') as notify_date,cms_document_archiving.attachment,cms_employees.name as emp_name,cms_employees.office_email FROM cms_document_archiving
			          INNER JOIN cms_employees on cms_document_archiving.created_by = cms_employees.id WHERE cms_document_archiving.notify_by <= CURDATE() AND cms_document_archiving.notify_by >= cms_document_archiving.from_date AND cms_document_archiving.notify_by <= cms_document_archiving.to_date AND cms_document_archiving.status_id = '205' AND cms_employees.is_active = 1 ORDER BY cms_employees.name ASC, cms_document_archiving.notify_by ASC
